<!-- OVERVIEW -->
<section id="overview">
  <div class="container reveal">
    <span class="section-label">Overview</span>
    <h2>The Architecture of <em>Narrative Control</em></h2>
    <p>This investigation maps every South African journalist currently holding a position at an international news outlet covering South Africa, and every major media house that shapes international perception of the country. The network is documented from publicly available bylines, LinkedIn profiles, Muck Rack records, and institutional staff pages.</p>
    <p>The map reveals three structural patterns that have not been documented elsewhere. The New York Times Johannesburg bureau, the single most influential node shaping United States elite opinion on South Africa, is staffed by three people: John Eligon (Bureau Chief, Trinidadian-American), Lynsey Chutel (reporter, SA-born, now London), and Joao Silva (photographer, Portuguese-born, raised SA). None speak Afrikaans. None are Afrikaner. The community most written about has no representation in the newsroom writing about it.</p>
    <p>The Open Society Foundation (OSF) funding pipeline surfaces through Latashia Naidoo (2020 Wits/OSF Investigative Journalism Fellow), connecting the journalist pipeline directly to the Africa Check, International Fact-Checking Network (IFCN), and Meta content moderation architecture documented in investigations 01, 03, and 04 of the Netwerk Leaks series.</p>
  </div>
</section>

<section id="map-section">

    <div style="padding:0 28px 16px;max-width:900px;margin:0 auto">
      <span class="section-label">Interactive 3D Network</span>
      <h2>The <em>Connections</em></h2>
      <p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-light)">Click any node to see its role, connections, and country of origin. Drag to rotate. Scroll to zoom. Media houses show brand badges. Journalists show country flags.</p>
    </div>

<!-- KEY PATTERNS -->
<section id="patterns">
  <div class="container">
    <span class="section-label reveal">Documented Patterns</span>
    <h2 class="reveal">What the <em>Network</em> Reveals</h2>

    <div class="pattern-grid">
      <div class="pattern reveal">
        <div class="tag">Bureau Control</div>
        <h4>The NYT Johannesburg Bureau</h4>
        <p>Three people control the entire New York Times visual and narrative output on South Africa: Eligon (Bureau Chief), Chutel (reporter), Silva (photographer). None are Afrikaner. None speak Afrikaans. Eligon quoted Max du Preez in his framing of white South Africans. Chutel co-authored "Coloured: How Classification Became Culture." The outlet with the most influence on US policy-makers has zero Afrikaans capacity.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="pattern reveal">
        <div class="tag">Revolving Door</div>
        <h4>The Lynsey Chutel Pipeline</h4>
        <p>eNCA (SA domestic), then Associated Press (wire service), then Quartz Africa, then News24 Africa desk (appointed under Hanns Seidel Foundation funding), then the New York Times. Each step escalates the platform while the journalist carries the same framing lens trained in the SA domestic ecosystem. Columbia Journalism MA. Wits International Relations (IR) MA. Connected to four outlets on the map.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="pattern reveal">
        <div class="tag">Funding Link</div>
        <h4>The OSF Fellowship Pipeline</h4>
        <p>Latashia Naidoo (2020 Wits/OSF Investigative Journalism Fellow, Thomson Reuters Changemaker 2021, BBC Komla Dumor Award finalist 2022) moved through eNCA, TRT World, BBC Africa, CNN, and Business Insider US before arriving at Carte Blanche. The OSF fellowship connects the journalist career pipeline to the Africa Check/IFCN/Meta content moderation architecture documented in Netwerk Leaks investigations 01 and 03.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="pattern reveal">
        <div class="tag">Break-Away</div>
        <h4>Lara Logan: The Exception</h4>
        <p>One SA-born journalist reached the top of international news and broke away. Lara Logan (Durban, 1971) rose through Reuters Television Africa (1992-1996), freelanced for ITN, Fox, Sky, CNN, ABC, and NBC, then served as CBS News Chief Foreign Affairs Correspondent from 2006 to 2018. She left CBS after challenging institutional framing. She is not on this network map because she left the network. That departure cost her career. No Afrikaner journalist has attempted the same path since. The system does not produce dissent. It filters it out.</p>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="finding reveal">
      <div class="finding-num">Finding 01</div>
      <h3>The SABC Pipeline</h3>
      <p>The South African Broadcasting Corporation (SABC) functions as a feeder institution for international careers. Robyn Curnow (CNN), Lerato Mbele (BBC), Redi Tlhabi (BBC), Haru Mutasa (Al Jazeera), Jane Dutton (Al Jazeera), Anand Naidoo (CGTN), and Sherwin Bryce-Pease (SABC UN Bureau) all transited through the state broadcaster before reaching international platforms. The SABC trains the voices. The international outlets select which voices reach global audiences.</p>
    </div>

    <div class="finding reveal">
      <div class="finding-num">Finding 02</div>
      <h3>The Afrikaans Media Silo</h3>
      <p>Netwerk24 (Naspers Afrikaans digital) has zero international connections. No Afrikaans journalist holds a position at CNN, BBC, Al Jazeera, Reuters, AFP, AP, the New York Times, the Guardian, CGTN, or ITV News. The Afrikaans press has no wire service connections. No fact-checking partnerships. No republication agreements. The language barrier is not just linguistic. It is structural, institutional, and complete.</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

<!-- KEY FINDING -->
<section id="finding-section" style="border-top:1px solid var(--border)">
  <div class="container" style="text-align:center">
    <span class="section-label reveal">Key Finding</span>
    <h2 class="reveal">The <em>Language Silo</em></h2>
    <p class="reveal" style="max-width:620px;margin:0 auto 16px;font-size:15px">Zero Afrikaans-speaking journalists hold positions at any international news outlet covering South Africa. Not one at CNN, the British Broadcasting Corporation (BBC), Al Jazeera, Reuters, the Associated Press (AP), Agence France-Presse (AFP), the New York Times, the Guardian, or France 24.</p>
    <p class="reveal" style="max-width:620px;margin:0 auto;font-size:15px">The community most written about internationally has no representation in the international newsrooms writing about it. This is documented structural exclusion.</p>
  </div>
</section>

  <div class="container">
    <div class="evidence-panel reveal">
      <div class="evidence-card">
        <h3>Editorial safety layer</h3>
        <p>This upgrade keeps the investigation forceful while reducing avoidable legal and ethical risk. The language now emphasises observable relationships, published affiliations, and interpretation boundaries.</p>
        <div class="risk-note"><strong>Important:</strong> Network proximity is not proof of coordination, misconduct, bias, or intent. It is a visual aid for source-led analysis.</div>
      </div>
      <div class="evidence-card">
        <h3>Verification checklist</h3>
        <ul class="verify-list">
          <li>Prefer primary biographies, outlet pages, and official institutional records.</li>
          <li>Label interpretation as analysis, not established fact.</li>
          <li>Avoid implying motive unless directly sourced.</li>
          <li>Keep correction channels visible and easy to use.</li>
        </ul>
      </div>

// Build edges
const ED=[];
ND.forEach(n=>{if(n.cn)n.cn.forEach(c=>ED.push([n.id,c]))});
[["ac","cnn_h"],["ac","bbc_h"],["ac","n24"],["ac","dm"],["dm","iss"],["dm","ama"],["conv","guardian_h"],["iol","cgtn_h"],["ac","ifcn"]].forEach(e=>ED.push(e));

// Categorise nodes for layout
const insM=ND.filter(n=>n.t==="m"&&!["ifcn","cnn_h","bbc_h","aje_h","afp_h","reuters_h","ap_h","nyt_h","guardian_h","cgtn_h","itv_h"].includes(n.id));
const insJ=ND.filter(n=>n.t==="j"&&n.cn&&n.cn.some(c=>insM.find(m=>m.id===c)));
const outM=ND.filter(n=>n.t==="m"&&!insM.includes(n));
const outJ=ND.filter(n=>n.t==="j"&&!insJ.includes(n));

// WIDER ring layout with more Y variation for depth
function ring(a,r,y,ySpread){a.forEach((n,i)=>{
  const ang=(i/a.length)*Math.PI*2+0.3;
  n._x=Math.cos(ang)*r;
  n._y=y+(Math.random()-0.5)*ySpread;
  n._z=Math.sin(ang)*r;
})}
ring(insM,12,0,3);
ring(insJ,24,2,4);
ring(outM,38,-1,5);
ring(outJ,52,1,6);

// THREE.JS
const cv=document.getElementById("cv"),ll=document.getElementById("ll");
const sc=new THREE.Scene();
sc.background=new THREE.Color(0x1B2A4A);
sc.fog=new THREE.FogExp2(0x1B2A4A,0.004);

const cam=new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(50,cv.clientWidth/cv.clientHeight,0.1,800);
cam.position.set(0,32,68);

const ren=new THREE.WebGLRenderer({canvas:cv,antialias:true});
ren.setSize(cv.clientWidth,cv.clientHeight);
ren.setPixelRatio(Math.min(devicePixelRatio,2));

// Soft lighting
sc.add(new THREE.AmbientLight(0xffffff,0.9));
const d1=new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xfff8ee,0.6);d1.position.set(20,30,25);sc.add(d1);
const d2=new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xeef0ff,0.35);d2.position.set(-15,10,-10);sc.add(d2);

// Very subtle ground grid
const gr=new THREE.GridHelper(140,35,0x2a3a5a,0x22324a);gr.position.y=-7;sc.add(gr);

// Ambient floating particles
const pGeo=new THREE.BufferGeometry();
const pCount=200;
const pPos=new Float32Array(pCount*3);
for(let i=0;i<pCount*3;i++)pPos[i]=(Math.random()-0.5)*120;
pGeo.setAttribute('position',new THREE.BufferAttribute(pPos,3));
const pMat=new THREE.PointsMaterial({color:0xC5A258,size:0.15,transparent:true,opacity:0.3,sizeAttenuation:true});
const particles=new THREE.Points(pGeo,pMat);
sc.add(particles);

// Create node meshes
const mM=new Map(),nM=new Map();
ND.forEach(nd=>{
  nM.set(nd.id,nd);
  if(nd._x===undefined)return;
  const r=nd.t==="m"?1.0+nd.w*0.18:0.55+nd.w*0.12;
  const c=new THREE.Color(nd.col);
  const mt=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:c,roughness:0.2,metalness:0.25,emissive:c,emissiveIntensity:0.25});
  const ms=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.SphereGeometry(r,32,32),mt);
  ms.position.set(nd._x,nd._y,nd._z);
  ms.userData=nd;
  sc.add(ms);
  mM.set(nd.id,ms);
});

// Colour-coded edges
const eL=[];
ED.forEach(([f,t])=>{
  const fm=mM.get(f),tm=mM.get(t);
  if(!fm||!tm)return;
  const g=new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints([fm.position.clone(),tm.position.clone()]);
  const fc=new THREE.Color(fm.userData.col);
  const ln=new THREE.Line(g,new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({color:fc,transparent:true,opacity:0.25,linewidth:1}));
  sc.add(ln);
  eL.push({line:ln,from:f,to:t});
});

// Build HTML labels with emoji flags + letter badges (ZERO external images)
const lbs=new Map();
ND.forEach(nd=>{
  if(nd._x===undefined)return;
  const d=document.createElement("div");
  d.className="nl"+(nd.t==="m"?" med":"");
  const flag=EF[nd.cc]||"";
  if(nd.t==="m"&&MB[nd.id]){
    const [code,bg]=MB[nd.id];
    d.innerHTML='<span class="bg" style="background:'+bg+'">'+code+'</span><img class="fi" src="'+flag+'"><span class="nm">'+nd.n+'</span>';
  }else{
    d.innerHTML='<img class="fi" src="'+flag+'"><span class="nm">'+nd.n+'</span>';
  }
  d.style.pointerEvents="auto";
  d.addEventListener("click",()=>openPanel(nd));
  ll.appendChild(d);
  lbs.set(nd.id,d);
});

// Camera orbit controls
let dr=false,pX=0,pY=0,rX=0,rY=0,tX=0,tY=0,zm=72;
cv.addEventListener("mousedown",e=>{dr=true;pX=e.clientX;pY=e.clientY});
cv.addEventListener("mousemove",e=>{if(!dr)return;tY+=(e.clientX-pX)*.004;tX+=(e.clientY-pY)*.004;tX=Math.max(-1.2,Math.min(1.2,tX));pX=e.clientX;pY=e.clientY});
cv.addEventListener("mouseup",()=>dr=false);
cv.addEventListener("mouseleave",()=>dr=false);
cv.addEventListener("wheel",e=>{e.preventDefault();zm=Math.max(30,Math.min(130,zm+e.deltaY*.06))},{passive:false});
cv.addEventListener("touchstart",e=>{if(e.touches.length===1){dr=true;pX=e.touches[0].clientX;pY=e.touches[0].clientY}});
cv.addEventListener("touchmove",e=>{if(!dr||e.touches.length!==1)return;tY+=(e.touches[0].clientX-pX)*.004;tX+=(e.touches[0].clientY-pY)*.004;tX=Math.max(-1.2,Math.min(1.2,tX));pX=e.touches[0].clientX;pY=e.touches[0].clientY});
cv.addEventListener("touchend",()=>dr=false);

// Click to select node
const ray=new THREE.Raycaster(),mo=new THREE.Vector2();
cv.addEventListener("click",e=>{
  const r=cv.getBoundingClientRect();
  mo.x=((e.clientX-r.left)/r.width)*2-1;
  mo.y=-((e.clientY-r.top)/r.height)*2+1;
  ray.setFromCamera(mo,cam);
  const h=ray.intersectObjects([...mM.values()]);
  if(h.length>0)openPanel(h[0].object.userData);
});

function openPanel(nd){
  const flag=EF[nd.cc]||"";
  const pB=document.getElementById("pB");
  if(nd.t==="m"&&MB[nd.id]){
    const [code,bg]=MB[nd.id];
    pB.style.background=bg;pB.textContent=code;pB.style.fontSize="11px";
  }else{
    pB.style.background="#888";pB.textContent=flag;pB.style.fontSize="20px";
  }
  document.getElementById("pF").innerHTML='<img src="'+flag+'" style="height:22px;border-radius:2px">';
  document.getElementById("pN").textContent=nd.n;
  document.getElementById("pR").textContent=(nd.t==="m"?"Media House":"Journalist")+" | "+nd.cc.toUpperCase();
  document.getElementById("pD").textContent=nd.desc||"";
  const tg=document.getElementById("pT");tg.innerHTML="";
  (nd.topics||[]).forEach(t=>{const s=document.createElement("span");s.className="ptg";s.textContent=t;tg.appendChild(s)});
  const cn=document.getElementById("pC");cn.innerHTML="";
  ED.filter(([f,t])=>f===nd.id||t===nd.id).forEach(([f,t])=>{
    const oid=f===nd.id?t:f;const o=nM.get(oid);if(!o)return;
    const d=document.createElement("div");d.className="pci";
    d.innerHTML='<img src="'+((EF[o.cc])||"")+'" style="height:11px;border-radius:1px;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:4px">'+o.n;
    d.onclick=()=>openPanel(o);cn.appendChild(d);
  });
  document.getElementById("pn").classList.add("open");
  // Highlight connected
  mM.forEach((m,id)=>{
    const c=ED.some(([f,t])=>(f===nd.id&&t===id)||(t===nd.id&&f===id))||id===nd.id;
    m.material.opacity=c?1:0.12;m.material.emissiveIntensity=c?0.4:0.08;m.material.transparent=!c;
  });
  eL.forEach(e=>{e.line.material.opacity=(e.from===nd.id||e.to===nd.id)?0.7:0.04});
}
function closePanel(){
  document.getElementById("pn").classList.remove("open");
  mM.forEach(m=>{m.material.opacity=1;m.material.transparent=false;m.material.emissiveIntensity=0.25;});
  eL.forEach(e=>{e.line.material.opacity=0.3});
}

// Legend
const le=document.getElementById("lg");
function aL(ti,ar){
  const h=document.createElement("h3");h.textContent=ti;le.appendChild(h);
  ar.forEach(nd=>{
    const d=document.createElement("div");d.className="li";
    const ch="#"+nd.col.toString(16).padStart(6,"0");
    const fl=EF[nd.cc]||"";
    d.innerHTML='<div class="ld" style="background:'+ch+'"></div><img src="'+fl+'" style="height:11px;border-radius:1px"><span>'+nd.n+'</span>';
    d.onclick=()=>openPanel(nd);
    le.appendChild(d);
  });
}
aL("Inside South Africa",[...insM,...insJ]);
aL("Outside South Africa",[...outM,...outJ]);

// Stats
document.getElementById("sJ").textContent=ND.filter(n=>n.t==="j").length;
document.getElementById("sM").textContent=ND.filter(n=>n.t==="m").length;
document.getElementById("sC").textContent=ED.length;
document.getElementById("sA").textContent="0";

// Animation loop
let ti=0;const v3=new THREE.Vector3();
function anim(){
  requestAnimationFrame(anim);
  ti+=0.004;
  rX+=(tX-rX)*0.04;rY+=(tY-rY)*0.04;
  cam.position.x=Math.sin(rY)*Math.cos(rX)*zm;
  cam.position.y=Math.sin(rX)*zm*0.4+20;
  cam.position.z=Math.cos(rY)*Math.cos(rX)*zm;
  cam.lookAt(0,0,0);
  // Gentle float
  // Animate particles
  if(particles){const pp=particles.geometry.attributes.position.array;
    for(let i=0;i<pp.length;i+=3){pp[i+1]+=0.005;if(pp[i+1]>30)pp[i+1]=-30;}
    particles.geometry.attributes.position.needsUpdate=true;
    particles.rotation.y=ti*0.05;}
  mM.forEach(m=>{const n=m.userData;if(n._y!==undefined)m.position.y=n._y+Math.sin(ti+n._x*0.2)*0.25});
  // Update edge positions
  eL.forEach(e=>{const f=mM.get(e.from),t=mM.get(e.to);if(f&&t){
    const p=e.line.geometry.attributes.position.array;
    p[0]=f.position.x;p[1]=f.position.y;p[2]=f.position.z;
    p[3]=t.position.x;p[4]=t.position.y;p[5]=t.position.z;
    e.line.geometry.attributes.position.needsUpdate=true;
  }});
  // Project labels to screen
  const cw=cv.clientWidth,ch=cv.clientHeight;
  lbs.forEach((d,id)=>{
    const m=mM.get(id);if(!m)return;
    v3.copy(m.position).project(cam);
    if(v3.z>1){d.style.display="none";return}
    d.style.display="flex";
    d.style.left=((v3.x*0.5+0.5)*cw)+"px";
    d.style.top=((-v3.y*0.5+0.5)*ch)+"px";
  });
  ren.render(sc,cam);
}
anim();

window.addEventListener("resize",()=>{
  cam.aspect=cv.clientWidth/cv.clientHeight;
  cam.updateProjectionMatrix();
  ren.setSize(cv.clientWidth,cv.clientHeight);
});

/* Scroll reveal */
const reveals=document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
const io=new IntersectionObserver((entries)=>{
  entries.forEach(e=>{if(e.isIntersecting){e.target.classList.add('visible')}});
},{threshold:0.1});
reveals.forEach(r=>io.observe(r));
</script>

<script>
(function(){
  document.body.classList.remove('no-js');
  const links=[...document.querySelectorAll('.nav-links a[href^="#"]')];
  const sections=links.map(a=>document.querySelector(a.getAttribute('href'))).filter(Boolean);
  const setCurrent=()=>{let current=null;for(const sec of sections){const r=sec.getBoundingClientRect();if(r.top<120) current=sec.id;} links.forEach(a=>a.setAttribute('aria-current',a.getAttribute('href')==='#'+current?'true':'false'));};
  setCurrent(); window.addEventListener('scroll',setCurrent,{passive:true});
  document.querySelectorAll('a[target="_blank"]').forEach(a=>{a.rel='noopener noreferrer';});
  document.querySelectorAll('.nl').forEach(el=>{el.setAttribute('tabindex','0'); el.setAttribute('role','button'); const name=el.textContent.trim(); if(name&&!el.getAttribute('aria-label')) el.setAttribute('aria-label','Open details for '+name); el.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{if(e.key==='Enter'||e.key===' '){e.preventDefault();el.click();}});});
  const search=document.getElementById('mapSearch'); const filter=document.getElementById('mapFilter'); const status=document.getElementById('mapStatus');
  function classify(el){const t=(el.textContent||'').toLowerCase(); if(el.classList.contains('med')||/bbc|cnn|reuters|guardian|afp|ap|nyt|al jazeera|daily maverick|news24|sabc|enca|media|outlet/.test(t)) return 'media'; if(/international|foreign|global/.test(t)) return 'international'; return 'journalist';}
  function applyMapFilters(){const q=(search?.value||'').trim().toLowerCase(); const f=filter?.value||'all'; let shown=0,total=0; document.querySelectorAll('.nl').forEach(el=>{total++; const txt=(el.textContent||'').toLowerCase(); const type=classify(el); const okText=!q||txt.includes(q); const okFilter=f==='all'||type===f||(f==='international'&&/(bbc|cnn|reuters|guardian|afp|ap|nyt|al jazeera|cgtn|itv)/.test(txt)); el.classList.toggle('filtered-out',!(okText&&okFilter)); if(okText&&okFilter) shown++;}); if(status) status.textContent= shown?`${shown} / ${total} nodes shown`:'No matching nodes';}
  search?.addEventListener('input',applyMapFilters); filter?.addEventListener('change',applyMapFilters); setTimeout(applyMapFilters,600);
  if(!window.THREE){const mw=document.getElementById('mw'); if(mw){mw.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin','<div class="risk-note" style="position:absolute;left:16px;right:16px;top:16px;z-index:30">3D engine unavailable. The written analysis and source list remain available below.</div>');}}
})();
</script>
